\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} Phase field class. It stores the phase fields, performs basic operations on them. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8h_source_l00047}{47}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8h_source}{Phase\+Field.\+h}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetMaxPhaseFieldOverlap()}{GetMaxPhaseFieldOverlap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ int $>$ openphase\+::\+Phase\+Field\+::\+Get\+Max\+Phase\+Field\+Overlap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{th\+Phase1,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{th\+Phase2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em th\+Phase1} & Returns a vector containing the phase indices th\+Phase1 and th\+Phase2 that have the biggest overlap, also the number of interface points between the phasefields. vector contains 1. phasefield of th\+Phase1, 2. phasefield of the\+Phase2, 3. number of overlap points. All values are -\/1 if no overlap is found. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void openphase\+::\+Phase\+Field\+::\+Keep\+Phase\+Volume\+DR (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1Tensor}{Tensor}}$<$ bool, 2 $>$}]{Allowed\+Transitions }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}

\Hypertarget{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField_afad83087d5475bb9d90d543b49ff7bb7}\label{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField_afad83087d5475bb9d90d543b49ff7bb7} 
\index{openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}!NormalizeIncrementsDR@{NormalizeIncrementsDR}}
\index{NormalizeIncrementsDR@{NormalizeIncrementsDR}!openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NormalizeIncrementsDR()}{NormalizeIncrementsDR()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void openphase\+::\+Phase\+Field\+::\+Normalize\+Increments\+DR (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1BoundaryConditions}{Boundary\+Conditions}} \&}]{BC,  }\item[{const double}]{dt }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Normalizes the interface fields such that resulting phase fields after merge do not escape interval \mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} and sum up to 1. 

This function limits phase-\/field increments for all present phase-\/field pairs, so that the actual phase-\/field values are within their natural limits of 0.\+0 and 1.\+0.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8cpp_source_l01634}{1634}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8cpp_source}{Phase\+Field.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField_afc48631e25443062d9fa47d59f793dc9}\label{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField_afc48631e25443062d9fa47d59f793dc9} 
\index{openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}!NormalizeIncrementsSR@{NormalizeIncrementsSR}}
\index{NormalizeIncrementsSR@{NormalizeIncrementsSR}!openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NormalizeIncrementsSR()}{NormalizeIncrementsSR()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void openphase\+::\+Phase\+Field\+::\+Normalize\+Increments\+SR (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1BoundaryConditions}{Boundary\+Conditions}} \&}]{BC,  }\item[{const double}]{dt }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



Normalizes the interface fields such that resulting phase fields after merge do not escape interval \mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} and sum up to 1. 

This function limits phase-\/field increments for all present phase-\/field pairs, so that the actual phase-\/field values are within their natural limits of 0.\+0 and 1.\+0.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8cpp_source_l01351}{1351}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8cpp_source}{Phase\+Field.\+cpp}}.

\index{openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}!WriteGrainsVolume@{WriteGrainsVolume}}
\index{WriteGrainsVolume@{WriteGrainsVolume}!openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{WriteGrainsVolume()}{WriteGrainsVolume()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void openphase\+::\+Phase\+Field\+::\+Write\+Grains\+Volume (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{time\+\_\+step,  }\item[{double}]{time,  }\item[{std\+::string}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Writes grains\textquotesingle{} volume in grid cells over time into a file. 

This function will write a list of all grain volumes in a file, each time this function is called in a new row. The first column is the time, the second row beginning with a "{}\#"{} marks the thermodynamic index for each grain.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8cpp_source_l02848}{2848}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{PhaseField_8cpp_source}{Phase\+Field.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField_ad31260709ab209458255a5f4d8541c3d}\label{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField_ad31260709ab209458255a5f4d8541c3d} 
\index{openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}!WriteVolumePercentages@{WriteVolumePercentages}}
\index{WriteVolumePercentages@{WriteVolumePercentages}!openphase::PhaseField@{openphase::PhaseField}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{WriteVolumePercentages()}{WriteVolumePercentages()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void openphase\+::\+Phase\+Field\+::\+Write\+Volume\+Percentages (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{filename,  }\item[{double}]{time,  }\item[{char}]{separator = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{},\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Writes volume fraction of all thermodynamic phases to the file File\+Name. 

This function will create tabulated data on the volume percent of each thermodynamic phase. Each time this function is called, a new row will be written in the specified file name for the current time step. If the file is not present it will be created, if the phase already exists, the new data will be appended!
